Why , home be the dear place in the world , and it should be the safe .
Just think how you would feel if you should be away from home , and then you should learn that it would n't be safe for you to go back there again , and you have no other place to go .
It often happen that way with the little people of the Green Meadows and the Green Forest .
It be that way with Happy Jack Squirrel now .
You see , Happy Jack know that Shadow the Weasel be not one to give up easily .
Shadow have one very good trait , and that be persistence .
He be not easily discourage .
When he set out to do a thing , usually he do it .
If he start to get a thing , usually he get it .
No , he be n't easily discourage .
Happy Jack know this .
No one know it good .
So Happy Jack do n't dare to go home .
He know that any minute of night or day Shadow might surprise him there , and that would be the end of him .
He more than half suspect that Shadow be at that very time hide somewhere along the way ready to spring out on him if he should try to go back home .
He have stay in the room of Farmer Brown 's boy until Mrs. Brown have come to make the bed .
Then he have jump out the window into the big maple tree .
He be n't quite sure of Mrs. Brown yet .
She have kindly eye .
They be just like the eye of Farmer Brown 's boy .
But he do n't feel really acquaint yet , and he felt safe outside than inside the room while she be there .
`` Oh dear , oh dear !
What shall I do ?
I have no home , and so To keep me warm and snug and safe I have no place to go ! ''
Happy Jack say this over and over a he sit in the maple tree , try to decide what be to be do .
`` I wonder what ail that Squirrel .
He seem to be do a lot of scolding , '' say Mrs. Brown , a she look out of the window .
And that show how easy it be to misunderstand people when we do n't know all about their affair .
Mrs. Brown think that Happy Jack be scold , when all the time he be just frighten and worry and wonder where he could go and what he could do to feel safe from Shadow the Weasel .
Because he do n't dare to go back to the Green Forest , he spend most of the day in the big maple tree close to Farmer Brown 's house .
The window have be close , so he could n't go inside .
He look at it longingly a great many time during the day , hop that he would find it open .
But he do n't .
You see , it be open only at night when Farmer Brown 's boy go to bed , so that he would have plenty of fresh air all night .
Of course Happy Jack do n't know that .
All his life he have have plenty of fresh air all the time , and be could n't understand how people could live in house all shut up .
Late that afternoon Farmer Brown 's boy , who have be at school all day , come whistle into the yard .
He notice Happy Jack right away .
`` Hello !
You back again !
Is n't one good meal a day enough ? ''
he exclaim .
`` He 's be there all day , '' say his mother , who have come to the door just in time to overhear him .
`` I do n't know what ail him . ''
Then Farmer Brown 's boy notice how forlorn Happy Jack look .
He remember Happy Jack 's fright that morning .
`` I know what 's the matter ! ''
he cry .
`` It 's that Weasel .
The poor little chap be afraid to go home .
We must see what we can do for him .
I wonder if he will stay if I make a new house for him .
I believe I 'll try it and see . ''
CHAPTER XXVIII HAPPY JACK FINDS A NEW HOME They say the very dark cloud Are line with silver bright and fair , Though how they know I do not see , And neither do I really care .
It 's good to believe , and so I try To believe 't be true with all my might , That nothing be so seeming dark But have a hidden side that 's bright .
Happy Jack .
Certainly thing could n't look much dark than they do to Happy Jack Squirrel a he sit in the big maple tree at the side of Farmer Brown 's house , and saw jolly , round , red Mr. Sun get ready to go to bed behind the Purple Hills .
He be afraid to go to his home in the Green Forest because Shadow the Weasel might be wait for him there .
He be afraid of the night which would soon come .
He be cold , and he be hungry .
Altogether he be a miserable a little Squirrel a ever be see .
He have just make up his mind that he would have to go look for a hollow in one of the tree in the Old Orchard in which to spend the night , when around the corner of the house come Farmer Brown 's boy with something under one arm and drag a ladder .
He whistle cheerily to Happy Jack a he put the ladder against the tree and climb up .
By this time Happy Jack have grow so timid that he be just a little afraid of Farmer Brown 's boy , so he climb a high up in the tree a he could get and watch what be go on below .
Even if he be afraid , there be comfort in have Farmer Brown 's boy near .
For some time Farmer Brown 's boy work busily at the place where the branch that Happy Jack know so well start out from the trunk of the tree towards the window of Farmer Brown 's boy 's room .
When he have fix thing to suit him , he go down the ladder and carry it away with him .
In the crotch of the tree he have leave the queer thing that he have bring under his arm .
In spite of his fear , Happy Jack be curious .
Little by little he creep nearer .
What he saw be a box with a round hole , just about big enough for him to go through , in one end , and in front of it a little shelf .
On the shelf be some of the nut that he like best .
For a long time Happy Jack look and look .
Was it a trap ?
Somehow he could n't believe that it be .
What would Farmer Brown 's boy try to trap him for when they be such good friend ?
At last the sight of the nut be too much for him .
It certainly be safe enough to help himself to those .
How good they taste !
Almost before he know it , they be go .
Then he get up courage enough to peep inside .
The box be fill with soft hay .
It certainly do look inviting in there to a fellow who have no home and no place to go .
He put his head inside .
Finally he go wholly in .
It be just as nice a it look .
`` I believe , '' think Happy Jack , `` that he make this little house just for me , and that he put all this hay in here for my bed .
He do n't know much about make a bed , but I guess he mean well . ''
With that he go to work happily to make up a bed to suit him , and by the time the first Black Shadow have creep as far a the big maple tree , Happy Jack be curl up fast asleep in his new house .
CHAPTER XXIX FARMER BROWN 'S BOY TAKES A PRISONER The craftiest and cleverest , the strong and the bold Will make mistake like other folk , young , middle-aged , and old .
Happy Jack .
Happy Jack Squirrel be happy once more .
He like his new house , the house that Farmer Brown 's boy have make for him and fasten in the big maple tree close by the house in which he himself live .
Happy Jack and Farmer Brown 's boy be get to be great friend than ever .
Every morning Happy Jack jump over to the window-sill and then in at the open window of the room of Farmer Brown 's boy .
There he be sure to find a good breakfast of fat hickory nut .
When Farmer Brown 's boy overslept , a he do sometimes , Happy Jack would jump up on the bed and waken him .
He think this great fun .
So do Farmer Brown 's boy , though sometimes when he be very sleepy he pretend to scold , especially on Sunday morning when he do not have to get up as early a on other day .
Of course , Black Pussy have soon discover that Happy Jack be live in the big maple tree , and she spend a great deal of time sit at the foot of it and glare up at him with a hungry look in her eye , although she be n't hungry at all , for she have plenty to eat .
Several time she climb up in the tree and try to catch him .
At first he have be afraid , but he soon find out that Black Pussy be not at all at home in a tree a he be .
After that , he rather enjoy have her try to catch him .
It be almost like a game .
It be great fun to scold at her and let her get very near him and then , just a she be sure that she be go to catch him , to jump out of her reach .
After a while she be content to sit at the foot of the tree and just glare at him .
Happy Jack have only one worry now , and this do n't trouble him a great deal .
It be possible that Shadow the Weasel might take it into his head to try to surprise him some night .
Happy Jack know that by this time Shadow must know where he be live , for of course Sammy Jay have find out , and Sammy be one of those who tell all he know .
Still , be so close to Farmer Brown 's boy give Happy Jack a very comfortable feeling .
Now all this time Farmer Brown 's boy have not forget Shadow the Weasel and how he have drive Happy Jack out of the Green Forest , and he have wonder a great many time if it would n't be a kindness to the other little people if he should trap Shadow and put him out of the way .
But you know he have give up trapping , and somehow he do n't like to think of set a trap , even for such a mischief-maker a Shadow .
Then something happen that make Farmer Brown 's boy very , very angry .
One morning , when he go to fee the biddy , he find that Shadow have visit the henhouse in the night and kill three of his best pullet .
That decide him .
He felt sure that Shadow would come again , and he mean to give Shadow a surprise .
He hunt until he find the little hole through which Shadow have get into the henhouse , and there he set a trap .
`` I do n't like to do it , but I 've get to , '' say he .
`` If he have be content with one , it would have be bad enough , but he kill three just from the love of killing , and it be high time that something be do to get rid of him . ''
The very next morning Happy Jack saw Farmer Brown 's boy come from the henhouse with something under his arm .
He come straight over to the foot of the big maple tree and put the thing he be carry down on the ground .
He whistle to Happy Jack , and a Happy Jack come down to see what it be all about , Farmer Brown 's boy grin .
`` Here 's a friend of yours you probably will be glad to see , '' say he .
At first , all Happy Jack could make out be a kind of wire box .
Then he saw something white inside , and it move .
Very suspiciously Happy Jack come nearer .
Then his heart give a great leap .
That wire box be a cage , and glare between the wire with red , angry eye be Shadow the Weasel !
He be a prisoner !
Right away Happy Jack be so excited that he act a if he be crazy .
He no longer have a single thing to be afraid of .
Do you wonder that he be excite ?
CHAPTER XXX A PRISONER WITHOUT FEAR A bad name be easy to get but hard to live down .
Happy Jack .
Shadow the Weasel be a prisoner .
He who always have be free to go and come a he please and to do a he please be now in a little narrow cage and quite helpless .
For once he have be careless , and this be the result .
Farmer Brown 's boy have catch him in a trap .
Of course , he should have know good than to have visit the henhouse a second time after kill three of the best pullet there .
He should have know that Farmer Brown 's boy would be sure to do something about it .
The truth be , he have yield to temptation when common sense have warn him not to .
So he have no one to blame for his present difficulty but himself , and he know it .
At first he have be in a terrible rage and have bite at the wire until he have make his mouth sore .
When he have make sure that the wire be stout than his teeth , he wisely stop try to get out in that way , and make up his mind that the only thing to do be to watch for a chance to slip out , if the door of the cage should happen to be leave unfastened .
Of course it hurt his pride terribly to be make fun of by those who always have fear him .
Happy Jack Squirrel be the first one of these to see him .
Farmer Brown 's boy have put the cage down near the foot of the big maple tree in which Happy Jack be live , because Shadow have drive him out of the Green Forest .
As soon a Happy Jack have make sure that Shadow really and truly be a prisoner and so quite harmless , he have act a if he be crazy .
Perhaps he be -- crazy with joy .
You see , he no longer have anything to be really afraid of , for there be no one but Shadow from whom he could not get away by run into his house .
Billy Mink be the only other one who could follow him there , and Billy be not likely to come climb up a tree so close to Farmer Brown 's house .
So Happy Jack race up and down the tree in the very great excitement , and his tongue go quite as fast a his leg .
He want everybody to know that Shadow be a prisoner at last .
At first he do not dare go very close to the cage .
You see , he have so long feared Shadow that he be still afraid of him even though he be so helpless .
But little by little Happy Jack grow bolder and come very close .
And then he begin do something not at all nice .
He begin call Shadow name and make fun of him , and tell him how he be n't afraid of him .
It be all very foolish and bad -- it be like hit a foe who be helpless .
Of course Happy Jack hasten to tell everybody he meet all about Shadow , so it be n't long before Shadow begin to receive many visitor .
Whenever Farmer Brown 's boy be not around there be sure to be one or more of the little people who have fear Shadow to taunt him and make fun of him .
Somehow it seem a if always it be that way when people get into trouble .
You know it be very easy to appear to be bold and brave when there be nothing to be afraid of .
Of course that be n't bravery at all , though many seem to think it be .
-LSB- Illustration : IT WAS N'T LONG BEFORE SHADOW BEGAN TO RECEIVE MANY VISITORS . -RSB-
Now what do you think that right down in their heart all these little people who come to jeer at Shadow the Weasel hop they would see ?
Why , they hop they would see Shadow afraid .
Yes , Sir , that be just what they hop .
But they do n't .
That be where they be disappoint .
Not once do Shadow show the least sign of fear .
He do n't know what Farmer Brown 's boy would do with him , and he have every reason to fear that if he be not to be keep a prisoner for the rest of his natural life , something dreadful would be the end .
But he be too proud and too brave to let any one know that any such fear ever enter his mind .
Whatever his fault , Shadow be no coward .
He boldly take bit of meat which Farmer Brown 's boy bring to him , and not once appear in the least afraid , so that , much a he dislike him , Farmer Brown 's boy actually have to admire him .
He be a prisoner , but he keep just a stout a heart a ever .
CHAPTER XXXI WHAT FARMER BROWN 'S BOY DID WITH SHADOW Ribble , dibble , dibble , dab !
Some people have the gift of gab !
Some people have no tongue at all To trip them up and make them fall .
Happy Jack .
It be a fact , one of the big fact in all the world , that tongue make the great part of all the trouble that bring uncomfortable feeling , and bitterness and sadness and suffering and sorrow .
If it be n't for unruly , careless , mean tongue , the Great World would be a million time well to live in , a million time happy .
It be because of his unruly tongue that Sammy Jay be forever get into trouble .
It be the same way with Chatterer the Red Squirrel .
And it be just the same way with a great many little boy and girl , and with grown-ups as well .
When the little people of the Green Forest and Green Meadows who fear Shadow the Weasel find that he be a prisoner , many of them take particular pain to visit him when the way be clear , just to make fun of him and tease him and tell him that they be not afraid of him and that they be glad that he be a prisoner , and that they be sure something dreadful would happen to him and they hop it would .
Shadow say never a word in reply .
He be too wise to do that .
He just turn his back on them .
But all the time he be store up in his mind all these hateful thing , and he mean , if ever he get free again , to make life very uncomfortable for those whose foolish tongue be try to make him more miserable than he already felt .
But these little people with the foolish tongue do n't stop to think of what might happen .
They just take it for grant that Shadow never again would run wild and free in the Green Forest , and so they just let their tongue run and enjoy do it .
Perhaps they would n't have , if they could have know just what be go on in the mind of Farmer Brown 's boy .
Ever since he have find Shadow in the trap which he have set for him in the henhouse , Farmer Brown 's boy have be puzzle over what he should do with his prisoner .
At first he have think he would keep him in a cage the rest of his life .
But somehow , whenever he look into Shadow 's fierce little eye and saw how unafraid they look , he get to think of how terrible it must be to be shut up in a little narrow cage when one have have all the Green Forest in which to go and come .
Then he think that he would kill Shadow and put him out of his misery at once .
`` He kill my pullet , and he be always hunt the harmless little people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows , so he deserve to be kill , '' think Farmer Brown 's boy .
`` He 's a pest . ''
Then he remember that after all Shadow be one of Old Mother Nature 's little people , and that he must serve some purpose in Mother Nature 's great plan .
Bad a he seem , she must have some use for him .
Perhaps it be to teach others through fear of him how to be smart and take good care of themselves and so be well fit to do their part .
The more he think of this , the harder it be for Farmer Brown 's boy to make up his mind to kill him .
But if he could n't keep him a prisoner and he could n't kill him , what could he do ?
He be scowl down at Shadow one morning and puzzling over this when a happy idea come to him .
`` I know what I 'll do ! ''
he exclaim .
Without another word he pick up the cage with Shadow in it and start off across the Green Meadows , which now , you know , be not green at all but cover with snow .
Happy Jack watch him out of sight .
He have go in the direction of the Old Pasture .
He be go a long time , and when he do return , the cage be empty .
Happy Jack blink at the empty cage .
Then he begin to ask in a scold tone , `` What do you do with him ?
What do you do with him ? ''
Farmer Brown 's boy just smile and toss a nut to Happy Jack .
And far up in the Old Pasture , Shadow the Weasel be once more free .
It be well for Happy Jack 's peace of mind that he do n't know that .
CHAPTER XXXII HAPPY JACK IS PERFECTLY HAPPY Never say a thing be so Unless you absolutely know .
Just remember every day To be quite sure of what you say .
Happy Jack .
Taking thing for grant do n't do at all in this world .
To take a thing for grant be to think that it be so without take the trouble to find out whether it be or not .
It be apt not only to get you yourself into trouble , but to make trouble for other people a well .
Happy Jack saw Farmer Brown 's boy carry Shadow the Weasel away in a cage , and he saw him bring back the cage empty .
What could he have do with Shadow ?
For a while he tease Farmer Brown 's boy to tell him , but of course Farmer Brown 's boy do n't understand Happy Jack 's language .
Now Happy Jack knew just what he would like to believe .
He would like to believe that Farmer Brown 's boy have take Shadow away and make an end of him .
And because he want to believe that , it be n't very hard to believe it .
There be the empty cage .
Of course Farmer Brown 's boy would n't have go to the trouble of trap Shadow unless he intend to get rid of him for good .
`` He 's make an end of him , that 's what he 's do ! ''
say Happy Jack to himself , because that be what he would have do if he have be in Farmer Brown 's boy 's place .
So have make up his mind that this be what have be do with Shadow , he at once tell all his friend that it be so , and be himself supremely happy .
You see , he felt that he no longer have anything to worry about .
Yes , Sir , Happy Jack be happy .
He like the house Farmer Brown 's boy have make for him in the big maple tree close by his own house .
He be sure of plenty to eat , because Farmer Brown 's boy always look out for that , and a a result Happy Jack be grow fat .
None of his enemy of the Green Forest dare come so near to Farmer Brown 's house , and the only one he have to watch out for at all be Black Pussy .
By this time he be n't afraid of her ; not a bit .
In fact , he rather enjoy tease her and get her to chase him .
When she be doze on the doorstep he like to steal very close , wake her with a sharp bark , and then race for the near tree , and there scold her to his heart 's content .
He have make friend with Mrs. Brown and with Farmer Brown , and he even felt almost friend with Bowser the Hound .
Sometimes he would climb up on the roof of Bowser 's little house and drop nutshell on Bowser 's head when he be asleep .
The funny thing be Bowser never seem to mind .
He would lazily open his eye and wink one of them at Happy Jack and thump with his tail .
He seem to feel that now Happy Jack be one of the family , just a he be .
So Happy Jack be just as happy a a fat Gray Squirrel with nothing to worry him could be .
He be so happy that Sammy Jay actually become jealous .
You know Sammy be a born trouble maker .
He visit Happy Jack every morning , and while he help himself to the good thing that he always find spread for him , for Farmer Brown 's boy always have something for the little feathered folk to eat , he would hint darkly that such goodness and kindness be not to be trust , and that something be sure to happen .
That be just the way with some folk ; they always be suspicious .
But nothing that Sammy Jay could say troubled Happy Jack ; and Sammy would fly away quite put out because he could n't spoil Happy Jack 's happiness the least little bit .
CHAPTER XXXIII SAMMY JAY UPSETS HAPPY JACK A good deed well do often be overlook , but you never be allow to forget a mistake .
Happy Jack .
Sammy Jay chuckle a he fly across the snow-covered Green Meadows on his way to his home in the Green Forest .
He chuckle and he chuckle .
To have hear him you would have think that either he have think of something very pleasant , or something very pleasant have happen to him .
Once he turn in the direction of Farmer Brown 's house , but change his mind a he saw the Black Shadows creep out from the Purple Hills , and once more head for the Green Forest .
`` Too late to-day .
Time I be home now .
It 'll keep until to-morrow , '' he mutter .
Then he chuckle , and he be still chuckle when he reach the big hemlock tree , among the thick branch of which he spend each night .
`` Do n't know what start me off to the Old Pasture this afternoon , but I 'm glad I go .
My , my , my , but I 'm glad I go , '' say he , a he fluff out his feather and prepare to tuck his head under his wing .
`` It pay to snoop around in this world and see what be go on .
I learn a long time ago not to believe everything I hear , and that the sure way to make sure of thing be to find out for myself .
Nothing like use my own eye and my own ear .
Well , I must get to sleep . ''
He begin to chuckle again , and he be still chuckle a he fell asleep .
The next morning Sammy Jay be astir at the very first sign of light .
He wait just long enough to see that every feather be in place , for Sammy be a bit vain , and very particular about his dress .
Then he head straight for Farmer Brown 's house .
Just a he expect he find Happy Jack Squirrel be awake , for Happy Jack be an early riser .
`` Good morning , '' say Sammy Jay , and try very hard to make his voice sound smooth and pleasant , a very hard thing for Sammy to do , for his voice , you know , be naturally harsh and unpleasant .
`` You seem to be look as happy a ever . ''
`` Of course I be , '' reply Happy Jack .
`` Why should n't I be ?
I have n't a thing to worry about .
Of course I 'm happy , and I hope you 're just as happy a I be .
I 'm go to get my breakfast now , and then I 'll be happy still . ''
`` That 's so .
There 's nothing like a good breakfast to make one happy , '' say Sammy Jay , help himself to some suet tie to a branch of the maple tree .
`` By the way , I saw an old friend of yours yesterday .
He inquire after you particularly .
He do n't exactly send his love , but he say that he hop you be as well and fat a ever , and that he will see you again some time .
He say that he do n't know of any one he like to look at good than you . ''
Happy Jack look flatter .
`` That be very nice of him , '' say he .
`` Who be it ? ''
`` Guess , '' reply Sammy .
Happy Jack scratch his head thoughtfully .
There be not many friend in winter .
Most of them be asleep or have go to the far away southland .
`` Peter Rabbit , '' he venture .
Sammy shake his head .
`` Jimmy Skunk ! ''
Again Sammy shake his head .
`` Jumper the Hare ! ''
`` Guess again , '' say Sammy , chuckle .
`` Little Joe Otter ! ''
`` Wrong , '' reply Sammy .
`` I give up .
Who be it ?
Do tell me , '' beg Happy Jack .
`` It be Shadow the Weasel ! ''
cry Sammy , triumphantly .
Happy Jack drop the nut he be just go to eat , and in place of happiness something very like fear grow and grow in his eye .
`` I -- I do n't believe you , '' he stammer .
`` Farmer Brown 's boy take him away and put an end to him .
I saw him take him . ''
`` But you do n't see him put an end to Shadow , '' declare Sammy , `` because he do n't .
He take him ` way up in the Old Pasture and let him go , and I saw him up there yesterday .
That 's what come of guess at thing .
Shadow be no more dead than you be .
Well , I must be go along .
I hope you 'll enjoy your breakfast . ''
With this , off fly Sammy Jay , chuckle a if he think he have do a very smart thing in upset Happy Jack , which go to show what queer idea some people have .
As for Happy Jack , he worry for a while , but a Shadow do n't come , and there be nothing else to worry about , little by little Happy Jack 's high spirit return , until he be as happy a ever .
And now , though he have have many adventure since then , I must leave him , for there be no more room in this book .
Perhaps if you ask him , he will tell you of these other adventure himself .
Meanwhile , bashful little Mrs. Peter Rabbit be anxious that you should know something about her .

I GENTLE SISTER SOUTH WIND ARRIVES `` Good news , good news for every one , above or down below , For Master Winsome Bluebird 's come to whistle off the snow ! ''
All the Green Meadows and all the Green Forest have hear the news .
Peter Rabbit have see to that .
And just as soon a each of the little meadow and forest folk hear it , he hurry out to listen for himself and make sure that it be true .
And each , when he hear that sweet voice of Winsome Bluebird , have kick up his heel and shout `` Hurrah ! ''
You see they all know that Winsome Bluebird never be very far ahead of gentle Sister South Wind , and that when she arrive , bluster , rough Brother North Wind be already on his way back to the cold , cold land where the ice never melt .
Of course Winsome Bluebird do n't really whistle off the snow , but after he come , the snow disappear so fast that it seem a if he do .
It be surprising what a difference a little good news make .
Of course nothing have really change that first day when Winsome Bluebird 's whistle be hear on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest , but it seem a if everything have change .
And it be all because that sweet whistle be a promise , a promise that every one knew would come true .
And so there be joy in all the heart on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest .
Even grim old Granny Fox felt it , and a for Reddy Fox , why , Reddy even shout good-naturedly to Peter Rabbit and hop he be feel well .
And then gentle Sister South Wind arrive .
She come in the night , and in the morning there she be , hard at work make the Green Meadows and the Green Forest ready for Mistress Spring .
She break the icy band that have bind the Smiling Pool and the Laughing Brook so long ; and the Smiling Pool begin to smile once more , and the Laughing Brook to gurgle and then to laugh and finally to sing merrily .
She touch the little bank of snow that remain , and straightway they melt and disappear .
She kiss the eight baby of Unc ' Billy Possum , and they kick off the bedclothes under which old Mrs. Possum have tuck them and scramble out of the big hollow tree to play .
She peep in at the door of Johnny Chuck and call softly , and Johnny Chuck awake from his long sleep and yawn and begin to think about get up .
She knock at the door of Digger the Badger , and Digger awake .
She tickle the nose of Striped Chipmunk , who be about half awake , and Striped Chipmunk sneeze and then he hop out of bed and hurry up to his doorway to shout good morning after her , a she hurry over to see if Bobby Coon be still sleep .
Peter Rabbit follow her about .
He could n't understand it at all .
Peter have smile to himself when he hear how softly she have call at the doorway of Johnny Chuck 's house , for many and many a time during the long winter Peter have stop at Johnny Chuck 's house and shout down the long hall at the top of his voice without once wake Johnny Chuck .
Now Peter nearly tumble over with surprise , a he hear Johnny Chuck yawn at the first low call of gentle Sister South Wind .
`` How do she do it ?
I do n't understand it at all , '' say Peter , a he scratch his long left ear with his long left hind leg .
Gentle Sister South Wind smile at Peter .
`` There be a lot of thing in this world that you will never understand , Peter Rabbit .
You will just have to believe them without understand them and be content to know that they be so , '' she say , and hurry over to the Green Forest to tell Unc ' Billy Possum that his old friend , Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , be on his way up from ol ' Virginny .
II JOHNNY CHUCK RECEIVES CALLERS The morning after gentle Sister South Wind arrive on the Green Meadows , Peter Rabbit come hop and skip down the Lone Little Path from the Green Forest .
Peter be happy .
He do n't know why .
He just be happy .
It be in the air .
Everybody else seem happy , too .
Peter have to stop every few minute just to kick up his heel and try to jump over his own shadow .
He have felt just that way ever since gentle Sister South Wind arrive .
`` I simply have to kick and dance !
I can not help but gaily prance !
Somehow I feel it in my toe Whenever gentle South Wind blow . ''
So sang Peter Rabbit a he hop and skip down the Lone Little Path .
Suddenly he stop right in the middle of the verse .
He sit up very straight and star down at Johnny Chuck 's house .
Some one be sit on Johnny Chuck 's door-step .
It look like Johnny Chuck .
No , it look like the shadow of Johnny Chuck .
Peter rub his eye and look again .

he cry .

he cry . -RSB-

III THE SINGERS OF THE SMILING POOL Mistress Spring be make everybody happy on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest and around the Smiling Pool .
With her gentle finger she waken one by one all the little sleeper who have spend the long winter dreaming of warm summer day and not know anything at all of rough , bluster Brother North Wind or Jack Frost .
As they waken , many begin to sing for joy .
But the clear , loud singer of all live in the Smiling Pool .
It be a long time before Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck know where they live .
Every night just before go to bed , Johnny Chuck would sit on his door-step just to listen , and a he listen somehow he felt well and happy ; and he always have pleasant dream after listen to the sweet singer of the Smiling Pool .
Even after he have curl himself up for the night deep down in his snug bedroom , he could hear those sweet voice , and whenever he wake up in the night he would hear them .
`` Spring !
Spring !
Spring !
Spring !
Beautiful , beautiful , beautiful Spring !
So gentle , so loving , so sweet and so fair !

Be happy !
Be joyful !

Spring !
Spring !
Spring !
Spring !

It be very mysterious .
Finally he ask Peter Rabbit if he know who the sweet singer be and where they be .

Peter be always willing to try to find out about thing he do n't already know about .

Spring !

There be no doubt about it this time ; those voice come right out of the water .

IV JOHNNY CHUCK FINDS OUT WHO THE SWEET SINGERS ARE Johnny Chuck could n't keep away from the Smiling Pool .
No , Sir , Johnny Chuck could n't keep away from the Smiling Pool .

And this be why he could n't keep away from the Smiling Pool .

They have n't dream of anything else .
So of course they go look for bird .
When they reach the Smiling Pool , the voice come right out of the water .
Johnny know that some bird , like many of the cousin of Mrs. Quack , can stay under water a long time , and so he do n't know but some other bird might .

V JOHNNY CHUCK BECOMES DISSATISFIED Johnny Chuck be unhappy .

Why be he unhappy ?
Well , he hardly know himself .
He have sleep comfortably all the long winter .
He have awaken very , very hungry , but now he have plenty to eat .
All about him the bird be sing or busily at work build new home .
And still Johnny Chuck felt unhappy .
It be dreadful to feel this way and not have any good reason for it .
One bright morning Johnny Chuck sit on his door-step watch Drummer the Woodpecker build a new home in the old apple-tree .
Drummer 's red head fly back and forth , back and forth , and his sharp bill cut out tiny bit of wood .
It be slow work ; it be hard work .
But Drummer seem happy , very happy indeed .
It be watch Drummer that start Johnny Chuck to think about his own home .
He have always think it a very nice home .
He have build it just a he want it .
From the doorstep he could look in all direction over the Green Meadows .
It have a front door and a hidden back door .
Yes , it be a very nice home indeed .
But now , all of a sudden , Johnny Chuck become dissatisfied with his home .
It be too near the Lone Little Path .
Too many people know where it be .
It be n't big enough .
The front door ought to face the other way .
Dear me , what a surprising lot of fault a discontented heart can find with thing that have always be just right !
It be so with Johnny Chuck .
That house in which he have spend so many happy day , which have protect him from all harm , of which he have be so proud when he first build it , be now the mean house in the world .
If other people have new house , why should n't he ?
The more he think about it , the more dissatisfied and discontent he become and of course the more unhappy .
You know one can not be dissatisfy and discontent and happy at the same time .
Now dissatisfy and discontent people be not at all pleasant to have around .
Johnny Chuck have always be one of the best natured of all the little meadow people , and everybody like him .

VI JOHNNY CHUCK TURNS TRAMP Johnny Chuck have turn tramp .
Yes , Sir , Johnny Chuck have turn tramp .

And then , almost without think what he be do , he have tell Jimmy Skunk that he could have the house he have work so hard to build the summer before and of which he have be so proud .
Then Johnny Chuck have swagger away down the Lone Little Path without once look back at the home he be leave .

He be go to see the world , and perhaps when he have see the world , he would build him a new house .

But right down in his heart Johnny Chuck do n't feel half so bold a he pretend .

You see , he have make up his mind that no matter what happen , he would n't come back , after have give his house to Jimmy Skunk .

It be a very brave little song , but Johnny Chuck do n't feel half so brave and bold a he try to think he do .

Then he think of old Whitetail the Marshhawk , who have give him such a fright and have so nearly catch him when he be a little fellow .

A great fear take possession of Johnny Chuck , and he make himself as flat a possible in the grass , for there be no place to hide .

But he do n't offer to touch him .
Indeed , it seem to Johnny that old Whitetail actually grin and wink at him .
And right then all his fear leave him .

`` Who 's afraid of him ! ''
He suddenly realize that he be no long a helpless little Chuck who could n't take care of himself , but big and strong , with sharp teeth with which his old enemy have no mind to make a close acquaintance , when there be mouse and snake to be catch without fight .
So he puff out his chest and go on , and actually begin to enjoy himself , and almost wish for a chance to show how big and strong he be .
VII JOHNNY 'S FIRST ADVENTURE After old Whitetail the Marshhawk pass Johnny Chuck without offer to touch him , Johnny begin to feel very brave and bold and important .
He strut and swagger along as much a his short leg would let him .

He forget the terrible lonesome feeling of a little while before .

In fact , he felt a if he would n't care if he never have another home .
Yes , Sir , that be the way that Johnny Chuck felt .
Do you know why ?
Just because he have just begin to realize how big and strong he really be .
Now it be a splendid thing to feel big and strong and brave , a very splendid thing !
But it be a bad thing to let that feel turn to pride , foolish pride .
Of course old Whitetail have n't really be afraid of Johnny Chuck .
He have simply pass Johnny with a wink , because there be plenty to eat without the trouble of fighting , and Whitetail do n't fight just for the fun of it .
But foolish Johnny Chuck really think that old Whitetail be afraid of him .
The more he think about it , the more tickle he felt and the more puffed up he felt .

There be a strange Chuck glaring at him from behind a little bunch of grass .
He be a big , gray old Chuck whom Johnny never have see on the Green Meadows before , and he do n't look the least bit afraid .
No , Sir , he do n't look the teeny , weeny bit afraid !
Somehow , Johnny Chuck do n't feel half so big and strong and brave a he have a few minute before .
But it would n't do to let this stranger know it .
Of course not !
So , though he felt very small inside , Johnny make all his hair bristle up and try to look very fierce .
`` Who be you and what be you do on my Green Meadows ? ''
he demand .
`` Your Green Meadows !
Your Green Meadows !
Ho , ho , ho !
Your Green Meadows ! ''
The stranger laugh an unpleasant laugh .
`` How long since you own the Green Meadows ?
I have just come down on to them from the Old Pasture , and I like the look of them so well that I think I will stay .
So run along , little boaster !
There be n't room for both of u here , and the sooner you trot along the good . ''
The stranger suddenly show all his teeth and grit them unpleasantly .
Now when Johnny Chuck hear this , great anger fill his heart .
A stranger have order him to leave the Green Meadows where he have be bear and always live !
He could hardly believe his own ear .
He , Johnny Chuck , would show this stranger who be master here !
With a squeal of rage , Johnny sprang at the gray old Chuck .
Then begin such a fight a the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind have never see before .
They dance around excitedly and cry : `` How dreadful ! ''
and hop that Johnny Chuck would win , for you know they love him very much .
Over and over the two little fighter roll , bite and scratch and tear and growl and snarl .
Jolly , round , red Mr. Sun hide his face behind a cloud , so a not to see such a dreadful sight .
The stranger have be in many fight and he be very crafty .
For a while Johnny felt that he be get the bad of it , and he begin to wonder if he really would have to leave the Green Meadows .
The very thought fill him with new rage and he fight hard than ever .
Now the stranger be old and his teeth be wear , while Johnny be young and his teeth be very sharp .
After a long , long time , Johnny felt the stranger grow weak .
Johnny fight hard than ever .
At last the stranger cry `` Enough ! ''
and when he could break away , start back towards the Old Pasture .
Johnny Chuck have win !
VIII JOHNNY HAS ANOTHER ADVENTURE Johnny Chuck lay stretch out on the cool , soft grass of the Green Meadows , pant for breath .
He be very tired and very sore .
His face be scratch and bite .
His clothes be tear , and he smart dreadfully in a dozen place .
But still Johnny Chuck be happy .
When he raise his head to look , he could see a gray old Chuck limp off towards the Old Pasture .
Once in a while the gray old Chuck would turn his head and show his teeth , but he keep right on towards the Old Pasture .
Johnny Chuck smile .
It have be a great fight , and more than once Johnny Chuck have think that he should have to give up .
He think of this now , and then he think with shame of how he have brag and boast just before the fight .
What if he have lose ?
He resolve that he would never again brag or boast .
But he also make up his mind that if any one should pick a quarrel with him , he would show that he be n't afraid .
It be get late in the afternoon when Johnny finally felt rest enough to go on .
He have get to find a place to spend the night .
He hobble along , for he be very stiff and sore , until he come to the edge of the Green Meadows , where they meet the Green Forest .
Jolly , round , red Mr. Sun be almost ready to go down to his bed behind the Purple Hills .
Shadows be already begin to creep through the Green Forest .
Somehow they give Johnny Chuck that same lonesome feeling that he have have when he first leave his old home .
You see he have always live out in the Green Meadows and somehow he be afraid of the Green Forest in the night .
So , instead of go into the Green Forest , he wander along the edge of it , look for a place in which to spend the night .
At last he come to a hollow log lie just out on the edge of the Green Meadows .
Very carefully Johnny Chuck examine it , to be sure that no one else be use it .
`` It 's just the place I 'm look for ! ''
he say aloud .
Just then there be a sharp hiss , a very fierce hiss .
Johnny Chuck felt the hair on his neck rise a it always do when he hear that hiss , and he be n't at all surprised , when he turn his head , to find Mr. Blacksnake close by .
Mr. Blacksnake glide swiftly up to the old log and coil himself in front of the opening .
Then he raise his head and run out his tongue in the most impudent way .
`` Run along , Johnny Chuck !
I 've decide to sleep here myself to-night ! ''
he say sharply .
Now when Johnny Chuck be a very little fellow , he have be in great fear of Mr. Blacksnake , a he have have reason to be .
And because he do n't know any good , he have be afraid ever since .
Mr. Blacksnake know this and so now he look as ugly a he know how .
But you see he do n't know about the great fight that Johnny Chuck have just win .
Now to win an honest fight always make one feel very strong and very sure of oneself .
Johnny look at Mr. Blacksnake and saw that Mr. Blacksnake do n't look half as big a Johnny have always think he do .
He make up his mind that a he have find the old log first , he have the best right to it .
`` I find it first and I 'm go to keep it ! ''
snap Johnny Chuck , and with every hair on end and grit his teeth , he walk straight towards Mr. Blacksnake .
Now Mr. Blacksnake be a great bluffer , while at heart he be really a coward .
With a fierce hiss he rush right at Johnny Chuck , expect to see him turn tail and run .
But Johnny stand his ground and show all his sharp teeth .
Instead of attack Johnny , Mr. Blacksnake glide past him and sneak away through the grass .
Johnny Chuck chuckle a he creep into the hollow log .
`` Only a coward run away without fight , '' he murmur sleepily .
IX ANOTHER STRANGE CHUCK Johnny Chuck awoke just a jolly , round , red Mr. Sun pull his own nightcap off .
At first Johnny could n't think where he be .
He blink and blink .
Then he roll over .

cry Johnny Chuck .
You see he be so stiff and sore from his great fight the day before , that it hurt to roll over .
But when he felt the smart of those wound , he remember where he be .
He be in the old hollow log that he have find on the edge of the Green Meadows just before dark .
It be the first time that Johnny have ever sleep anywhere , except underground , and a he lay blink his eye , it seem very strange and rather nice , too .
`` Well , well , well !
What be you do here ? ''
cry a sharp voice .
Johnny Chuck look towards the open end of the old log .
There , peep in , be a little face as sharp a the voice .
`` Hello , Chatterer ! ''
cry Johnny .
`` I say , what be you do here ? ''
persist Chatterer the Red Squirrel , for it be he .
`` Just wake up , '' reply Johnny , with a grin .
`` It 's time , '' reply Chatterer .
`` But that be n't tell me what you be do so far from home . ''
`` I have n't any home , '' say Johnny , his face grow just a wee bit wistful .
`` You have n't any home ! ''
Chatterer 's voice sound a if he do n't think he have hear aright .
`` What have you do with it ? ''
`` Given it to Jimmy Skunk , '' reply Johnny Chuck .
Now Chatterer never give anything to anybody , and how any one could give away his home be more than he could understand .
He star at Johnny a if he think Johnny have go crazy .
Finally he find his tongue .
`` I do n't believe it ! ''
he snap .
`` If Jimmy Skunk have get your old home , it 's because he put you out of it . ''
`` No such thing !
I 'd like to see Jimmy Skunk or anybody else put me out of my home ! ''
Johnny Chuck speak scornfully .
`` I give it to him because I do n't want it any longer .
I 'm go to see the world , and then I 'm go to build me a new home .
Everybody else seem to be build new home this spring ; why should n't I ? ''
`` I 'm not ! ''
retort Chatterer .
`` I know enough to know when I be well off .
`` Who have a discontented heart Is sure to play a sorry part . ''
Johnny Chuck crawl out of the old log and stretch himself somewhat painfully .
`` That may be , but there be different kind of discontent .
Who never look for good thing Will live his life in little ring .
Well , I must be move along , if I be to see the world . ''
So Johnny Chuck bid Chatterer good-by and start on .
It be very delightful to wander over the Green Meadows on such a beautiful spring morning .
The violet and the wind-flowers nod to him , and the dandelion smile up at him .
Johnny almost forget his torn clothes and the bite and scratch of his great fight with the gray old Chuck the day before .
It be fun to just go where he please and not have a care in the world .
He be think of this , a he sit up to look over the Green Meadows .
His heart give a great throb .
What be that over near the lone elm - tree ?
It be -- yes , it certainly be another Chuck !
Could it be the old gray Chuck come back for another fight ?
A great anger fill the heart of Johnny Chuck , and he whistle sharply .
The strange Chuck do n't answer .
Johnny grind his teeth and start for the lone elm-tree .
He would show this other Chuck who be master of the Green Meadows !
X WHY JOHNNY CHUCK DID N'T FIGHT Anger be an awful thing ; It never stop to reason .
It boil right over all at once , No matter what the season .
It be so with Johnny Chuck .
The minute he catch sight of the strange Chuck over by the lone elm-tree , anger fill his heart and fairly boil over , until he be in a terrible rage .
Of course it be foolish , very foolish indeed .
The strange Chuck have n't say or do anything to make Johnny Chuck angry , not the least thing in the world , except to come down on to the Green Meadows .
Now the Green Meadows be very broad , and there be room for many Chucks .
It be pure selfishness on the part of Johnny Chuck to want to drive away every other Chuck .
But anger never stop to reason .
It do n't now .
Johnny Chuck hurry a fast a his short leg could take him towards the lone elm-tree , and in his mind be just one thought -- to drive that strange Chuck off the Green Meadows and to punish him so that he never , never would dare even think of come back .
So great be Johnny 's anger that every hair stand on end , and a he run he chatter and scold .
`` I 'll fix him !
These be my Green Meadows , and no one else have any business here unless I say so !
I 'll fix him !
I 'll fix him ! ''
Then Johnny would grind his teeth , and in his eye be the ugly look .
He be n't nice to see , not a bit nice .
The Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind do n't know what to make of him .
Could this be the Johnny Chuck they have know so long , the good-natured , happy Johnny Chuck whom everybody love ?
They draw away from him , for they do n't want anything to do with any one in such a frightful temper .
But Johnny Chuck do n't even notice , and if he have he would n't have care .
That be the trouble with anger .
It crowd out everything else , when it once fill the heart .
When Johnny have first see the stranger , he have think right away that it be the old gray Chuck with whom he have have such a terrible fight the day before and whom he whip .
Perhaps that be one reason for Johnny Chuck 's terrible anger now , for the old gray Chuck have try to drive Johnny Chuck off the Green Meadows .
But when he have to stop for breath and sit up to look again , he saw that it be n't the old gray Chuck at all .
It be a young Chuck and much small than the old gray Chuck .
It be small than Johnny himself .
`` He 'll be all the easy to whip , '' mutter Johnny , a he start on again , never once think of how unfair it would be to fight with one small than himself .
That be because he be so angry .
Anger never be fair .
Pretty soon he reach the lone elm-tree .
The stranger be n't to be see !
No , Sir , the stranger be n't anywhere in sight .
Johnny Chuck sit up and look this way and look that way , but the stranger be nowhere in sight .
`` Pooh ! ''
say Johnny Chuck , `` He 's afraid to fight !
He 's a coward .
But he ca n't get away from me so easily .
He 's hiding , and I 'll find him and then -- '' Johnny do n't finish , but he grind his teeth , and it be n't a pleasant sound to hear .
So Johnny Chuck hunt for the stranger , and the longer he hunt the angrier he grow .
Somehow the stranger manage to keep out of his sight .
He be almost ready to give up , when he almost stumble over the stranger , hide in a little clump of bush .
And then a funny thing happen .
What do you think it be ?
Why , all the anger leave Johnny Chuck .
His hair no longer stand on end .
He do n't know why , but all of a sudden he felt foolish , very foolish indeed .
`` Who be you ? ''
he demand gruffly .
`` I -- I 'm Polly Chuck , '' reply the stranger , in a small , timid voice .
XI THE GREATEST THING IN THE WORLD Johnny Chuck have begin to think about his clothes .
Yes , Sir , he spend a whole lot of time think about how he look and wish that he have a handsomer coat .
For the first time in all his life he begin to envy Reddy Fox , because of the beautiful red coat of which Reddy be so proud .
It seem to Johnny that his own coat be so plain and so dull that no one would look at it twice .
Besides , it be tear now , because of the great fight Johnny have have with the old gray Chuck who come down from the Old Pasture .
Johnny smooth it down and brush it carefully and try to make himself look a spick and span a he know how .
`` Oh , dear ! ''
he sigh .
`` I do n't see why Old Mother Nature do n't give me a handsome a coat a she do Reddy Fox .
And there be Jimmy Skunk and Happy Jack the Gray Squirrel and -- and -- why , almost every one have a handsomer coat than I have ! ''
Now this be n't at all like Johnny Chuck .
First he have be discontent with his house and have give it to Jimmy Skunk .
Now he be discontent with his clothes .
What be come over Johnny Chuck ?
He really do n't know himself .
At least , he would n't have admit that he know .
But right down deep in his heart be a great desire -- the desire to have Polly Chuck admire him .
Yes , Sir , that be what it be !
And it seem to him that she would admire him a great deal more if he wear fine clothes .
You see , he have n't learn yet what Peter Rabbit have learn a long time ago , which be that Fine clothes but catch the passing eye ; Fine deeds win love from low and high .
So Johnny Chuck wish and wish that he have a handsome suit , but a he do n't , and no amount of wish would bring him one , he just make the one he do have look as good a he could , and then go in search of Polly Chuck .
Sometimes she would not notice him at all .
Sometimes he would find her shyly peeping at him from behind a clump of grass .
Then Johnny Chuck would try to make himself look very important , and would strut about as if he really do own the Green Meadows .
Sometimes she would hide from him , and when he find her she would run away .
Other time she would be just a nice to him a she could be , and they would have a jolly time hunt for sweet clover and other nice thing to eat .
Then Johnny Chuck 's heart would swell until it seem to him that it would fairly burst with happiness .
Instead of want to drive Polly Chuck away from the Green Meadows , a he have the old gray Chuck , Johnny begin to worry for fear that Polly Chuck might not stay on the Green Meadows .
Whenever he think of that , his heart would sink way , way down , and he would hurry to look for her and make sure that she be still there .
When he be beside her , he felt very big and strong and brave and long for a chance to show her how brave he be .
She be such a timid little thing herself that the least little thing frighten her , and Johnny Chuck be glad that this be so , for it give him a chance to protect her .
When he be n't with her , he spend his time look for new patch of sweet clover to take her to .
At first she would n't go without a great deal of coaxing , but after a while he do n't have to coax at all .
She seem to delight to be with him as much a he do to be with her .
So Johnny Chuck grow happy and happy .
He be happy than he have ever be in all his life before .
You see Johnny Chuck have find the great thing in the world .
Do you know what it be ?
It be call love .
XII JOHNNY CHUCK PROVES HIS LOVE These spring day be beautiful day on the Green Meadows .
It seem to Johnny Chuck that the Green Meadows never have be so lovely or the song of the bird so sweet .
He have forget all about his old friend , Jimmy Skunk and Peter Rabbit and the other little meadow people .
You see , he could n't think of anybody but Polly Chuck , and he do n't want to be with anybody but Polly Chuck .
He have even forget that he have start out to see the world .
He do n't care anything more about the world .
All he want be to be where Polly Chuck be .
Then he be perfectly happy .
That be because Johnny Chuck have find the great thing in the world , which be love .
But Johnny still have one great wish , the wish that he might show Polly Chuck just how brave and strong he be and how well he could take care of her .
One morning they be feast in a patch of sweet clover over near an old stone wall .
It be the same stone wall in which Johnny Chuck have escape from old Whitetail the Marshhawk , when Johnny be a very little fellow .
Suddenly Polly give a little scream of fright .
Johnny Chuck look up to see a dog almost upon her .
Johnny 's first thought be to run to the old stone wall .
He be nearer to it than Polly be .
Then he saw that that dreadful dog would catch Polly before she could reach the stone wall .
A great rage fill Johnny 's heart , just a it have when he have fight the old gray Chuck .
Every hair stand on end , not with fear , but with anger , and he spring in front of Polly .
`` Run , Polly , run ! ''
he cry , and Polly run .
But Johnny do n't run .
Oh , my , no !
Johnny do n't run .
He draw himself together ready to spring .
He show all his sharp teeth and grind them savagely .
Little spark of fire seem to snap out of his eye .
There be no sign of fear in Johnny Chuck then , not the least little bit .
Just in front of him the dog stop and bark .
He be a little dog , a young and foolish dog , and he be terribly excite .
He bark until he almost lose his breath .
He do n't like the look of Johnny Chuck 's sharp teeth .
So he circle around Johnny , try to get behind him .
But Johnny turn a the dog circle , and always the little dog find those sharp teeth directly in front of him .
He bark and bark , until it seem a if he would bark his head off .
Finally the little dog , who be young and foolish , grow tire of just dance around and bark .
`` Pooh ! ''
say he to himself .
`` He 's nothing but a Chuck ! ''
Then he stop bark and sprang straight at Johnny with an ugly growl .
Johnny Chuck be ready for him and he be quick than the little dog .
His sharp teeth close on one of the little dog 's ear , and he hold on while with his stout claw he scratch and tore .
The little dog , who be young and foolish and have n't yet learn how to fight , could n't get hold of Johnny Chuck anywhere .
Then he try to shake Johnny Chuck off , but he could n't , because Johnny hold on to that ear with his sharp teeth .
`` Kiyi-yi-yi-yi ! ''
yell the little dog , for those teeth hurt dreadfully .
`` Kiyi-yi-yi-yi ! ''
Over and over they roll and tumble , the little dog try to get away , and Johnny Chuck hold on to the little dog 's ear .
Finally Johnny have to let go to get his breath .
The little dog sprang to his foot and start for home across the Green Meadows as fast a he could run .
Johnny Chuck shake himself and grin , a he hear the little dog 's `` Kiyi-yi-yi '' grow fainter and fainter .
`` I 'm glad it be n't Bowser the Hound , '' mutter Johnny Chuck , a he start towards the old stone wall .
There he find Polly Chuck peep out at him , and all of a tremble with fright .
`` My , how brave you be ! ''
say Polly Chuck .
`` Pooh , that 's nothing ! ''
reply Johnny Chuck .
XIII POLLY AND JOHNNY CHUCK GO HOUSE HUNTING Johnny Chuck be happy .
Yes , Sir , Johnny Chuck be happy -- so happy that he felt like do foolish thing .
You see Johnny Chuck love Polly Chuck and he know now that Polly Chuck love him .
He have know it ever since he have fight with the foolish little dog who have dare to frighten Polly Chuck .
After the fight be over , and the little dog have be send home kiyi - yi-ing , Polly Chuck have creep out of the old stone wall where she have be hide and snuggle up beside Johnny Chuck and look at him a if she think him the most wonderful Chuck in all the world , a , indeed , she do .
And Johnny have felt his heart swell and swell with happiness until it almost choke him .
So now once more Johnny Chuck begin to think of a new home .
He have forget all about see the world .
All he want now be a new house , build just so , with a front door and a hidden back door , and big enough for two , for no more would Johnny Chuck live alone .
So , with shy little Polly Chuck by his side , he begin to search for a place to make a new home .
The more he think about it , the more Johnny want to build his house over by the lone elm-tree where he have first see Polly Chuck .
It be a splendid place .
From it you could see a great way in every direction .
It would be shady on hot summer day .
It be near a great big patch of sweet clover .
It seem to Johnny Chuck that it be the best place on all the Green Meadows .
He whisper as much to Polly Chuck .
She turn up her nose .
`` It 's too low ! ''
say she .
`` Oh ! ''
reply Johnny , and look puzzle , for really it be one of the high place on the Green Meadows .
`` Yes , '' say Polly , in a brisk , decide way , `` it 's altogether too low .
Probably it be wet . ''
`` Oh ! ''
say Johnny once more .
Of course he know that it be n't wet , but if Polly do n't want to live there , he would n't say a word .
Of course not .
`` Now there 's a place right over there , '' continue Polly .
`` I think we 'll build our house right there . ''
Johnny open his mouth to say something , but he close it again without speaking and meekly trot after Polly Chuck to the place she have pick out .
It be in a little hollow .
Johnny know before he begin to dig that the ground be damp , almost wet .
But if Polly want to live there she should , and Johnny begin to dig .
By and by he stop to rest .
Where be Polly ?
He look this way and that way anxiously .
Just a he be get ready to go hunt for her , she come hurry back .
-LSB- Illustration : If Polly want to live there she should -RSB- `` I 've find a perfectly lovely place for our new home ! ''
she cry .
Johnny look ruefully at the hole he have work so hard to dig ; then he brush the dirt from his clothes and follow her .
This time Johnny have no fault to find with the ground .
It be high and dry .
But Polly have choose a spot close to a road that wind down across the Green Meadows .
Johnny shake his head doubtfully , but he begin to dig .
This time , however , he keep one eye on Polly Chuck , and the minute he find that she be wander off , he stop dig and chuckle a he watch her .
It be n't long before back she come in great excitement .
She have find a good place !
So they wander over the Green Meadows , Polly lead the way .
Johnny have learn by this time to waste no time dig .
And he have make up his mind to one thing .
What do you think it be ?
It be this : He would follow Polly until she find a place to suit him , but when she do find such a place she should n't have a chance to change her mind again .
XIV A NEW HOME AT LAST Home , no matter where it be , Or it be big or small , Is just the one place in the world That dearest be of all .
Johnny Chuck be think of this a he work with might and main .
It be a new house that he be build , but already he felt that it be home , and every time he think of it he felt a queer little tugging at his heart .
You see , while it be his home , it be Polly Chuck 's home , too , and that make it doubly dear to Johnny Chuck , even before it be finish .
And where do you think Johnny be build his new home ?
It be clear way over on the edge of Farmer Brown 's old orchard !
Yes , Sir , after all the fuss Johnny Chuck have make over any other Chuck living on the Green Meadows , and after drive the old gray Chuck back to the Old Pasture , Johnny Chuck have leave the Green Meadows himself !
It be n't of his own accord that Johnny Chuck have leave the Green Meadows .
No , indeed !
He love them too well for that .
But he love Polly Chuck more , and although he have grumble a little , he have follow her up to the old orchard , and now they be go to stay there .
Sometimes Johnny shiver when he think how near be Farmer Brown and Farmer Brown 's boy and Bowser the Hound .
He have never be so far from his old home on the Green Meadows before , and it be all very strange up here .
It be very lovely , too .
Besides , it be in this very old orchard that Polly Chuck have be bear , and she know every part of it .
Johnny felt well when he find that out .
So he set to work to build a home , and this time he mean business .
Polly Chuck could change her mind a many time a she please ; that be go to be their home and that be where they be go to live .
Now Johnny Chuck have grow wise in the way of the world since he first run away from the home where he be bear .
Twice since then he have build a new home , and now this would be good than either of the others .
He pay no heed to Polly , when she pout because he do not dig where she want him to .
He go from tree to tree , big old apple - tree they be , and at the very last tree , way down in a corner near a tumbled-down stone wall , he find what he want -- two spread root give him a chance to dig between them .
Polly watch him get ready for work and she pout some more .
`` It would be a lot nicer out in that grassy place , and a lot easy to dig , '' say she .
Johnny Chuck smile and make the dirt fly .
`` It certainly would be easy to dig , '' say he , when he stop for breath , `` easy for me and easy for Bowser the Hound or for old Granny Fox , if either want to dig u out .
Now , these old root be just far enough apart for u to go in and out .
They make a beautiful doorway .
But Bowser the Hound can not get through if he try , and he ca n't make our doorway any large .
Do n't you see how safe it be ? ''
Polly Chuck have to own up that it be safe than a home in the open could possibly be , and Johnny go on digging .
He make a long hall down to the snuggest of bedroom , deep , deep down under ground .
Then he make a long back hall , and all the sand from this he carry out the front way .
By and by he make a back door at the end of the back hall , and it open right behind a big stone fall from the old stone wall .
You would never have guess that there be a back door there .
His new house be finish now , and Johnny Chuck and Polly Chuck sit on the door-step and watch jolly , round , red Mr. Sun go to bed behind the Purple Hills and be happy .
XV SAMMY JAY FINDS THE NEW HOME Johnny Chuck be miss from his old home on the Green Meadows .
If he have know how much he be miss , he certainly would have try to go back for at least a call on his old neighbor .
There have be great surprise when it have be discover that Jimmy Skunk be live in Johnny 's old house , and at first some of the little meadow people be incline to look at Jimmy a wee bit distrustfully when he tell how Johnny Chuck have give away his house .
When Johnny send back word by the Merry Little Breezes that it be true , they believe Jimmy Skunk and forget the unpleasant thing that they have begin to hint at about him .
But they one and all think that Johnny Chuck must be crazy .
Yes , Sir , they think that Johnny Chuck must be crazy .
They be sure of it when the Merry Little Breezes bring word of how Johnny have start out to see the world .
But everybody be so busy about their own affair in the beautiful bright spring-time that they could n't spend much time wonder about Johnny Chuck .
They miss him every time they pass his old house and then forget him ; that be , most of the little meadow people do .
Peter Rabbit do n't .
Peter use to stop every day to gossip with Johnny Chuck and tell him all the news , and now that Johnny Chuck be no long there , Peter miss him greatly .
Jimmy Skunk be always asleep or off somewhere .
Besides , he be such a traveler that he know all the news almost as soon a Peter himself .
The Merry Little Breezes tell Peter that Johnny Chuck be still on the Green Meadows , hunt for a new home , so Peter make up his mind that just as soon a Johnny get settle , Peter would hunt him up and call .
You see , he never dream that Johnny would leave the Green Meadows , and he think that of course the Merry Little Breezes would tell him just where Johnny Chuck 's new house be , whenever it be build .
But there be where Peter make a mistake .
The Merry Little Breezes be the friend of all the little meadow and forest people , but they would n't be very long if they tell everything that they find out .
Their merry tongue they guard full well And thing they should n't never tell , For long ago they learn the way To keep a secret night and day .
And so when they find Johnny Chuck 's new house in the corner of Farmer Brown 's old orchard , they promise Johnny that they would n't tell anybody , and they do n't .
So it be a long time before any one else find out what have become of Johnny Chuck , for no one thought of look in the corner of the old orchard .
The Merry Little Breezes use to come every day and bring Johnny Chuck the news , and he and Polly Chuck would laugh and tickle , a they think of Peter Rabbit hunting and hunting and never find them .
Then one morning , a Johnny Chuck sit on his door-step , half dozing in the sun with his heart fill with contentment , he happen to look up straight into two sharp eye peer down at him from among the leaf of the apple-tree under which he have build his house .
He know those eye .
They be such sharp eye that they be unpleasant .
He do n't even have to look for the blue and white coat of the owner to know who have find his snug home .
But he pretend to keep right on dozing , and pretty soon the owner of the eye disappear without make a sound .
`` Oh , dear , '' sigh Johnny Chuck , `` now the whole world will know where we live , for that be Sammy Jay . ''
Then his face brighten a he add : `` Anyway , he do n't see Polly Chuck , and he do n't know anything about her , so I 'll keep twice as sharp a watch a before . ''
XVI SAMMY JAY PLANS MISCHIEF Mischief may not mean to be really truly bad , But somehow it seem to make other people sad ; Does a mean unpleasant thing and try to think it fun ; Then , ala , it run away when trouble have begin .
Of all the little people who live in the Green Forest and on the Green Meadows , none be more mischievous than Sammy Jay .
It seem sometimes a if there be more mischief under that pert little cap Sammy Jay wear than in the head of all the other little meadow and forest people put together .
When he be n't actually in mischief , Sammy Jay be plan mischief .
You see it have grow to be a habit with Sammy Jay , and habit , especially bad habit , have a way of grow and grow .
Now Sammy Jay have no quarrel with Johnny Chuck .
Oh , my , no !
He would have tell you that he like Johnny Chuck .
Everybody like Johnny Chuck .
But just as soon a Sammy Jay find Johnny Chuck 's new house , he begin to plan mischief .
He do n't really want any harm to come to Johnny Chuck , but he want to make Johnny uncomfortable .
That be Sammy Jay 's idea of fun -- see somebody else uncomfortable .
So he slip away to a thick hemlock-tree in the Green Forest to try to think of some plan to tease Johnny Chuck and make him uncomfortable .
Of course he know that Johnny have hide his new house in the corner of Farmer Brown 's old orchard because he want it to be a secret .
He do n't know why Johnny want it a secret and he do n't care .
If Johnny want it a secret , it would be fun to tell everybody about it .
As he sit wonder who he should tell first ; he saw Reddy Fox trot down the Lone Little Path .
`` Hi , Reddy Fox ! ''
he shout .
Reddy look up .
`` Hello , Sammy Jay !
What have you get on your mind this morning ? ''
say Reddy .
`` Nothing much , '' reply Sammy Jay .
`` What 's the news ? ''
Reddy grin .
`` There be n't any news , '' say he .
`` I be just go to ask you the same thing . ''
It be Sammy Jay 's turn to grin , `` Just a if I could tell you any news , Reddy Fox !
Just a if I could tell you any news ! ''
he exclaim .
`` Why , everybody know that you be so smart that you find out everything as soon a it happen . ''
Reddy Fox felt flatter .
You know people who do a great deal of flatter themselves be often the very easy to flatter if you know how .
Reddy pretend to be very modest ; but no one like to be think smart and important more than Reddy Fox do , and it please him greatly that Sammy Jay should think him so smart that no one could tell him any news .
Sammy know this perfectly well , and he chuckle to himself a he watch Reddy Fox pretend to be so modest .
`` Have you call on Johnny Chuck at his new home yet ? ''
ask Sammy Jay , in the most matter-of-fact way .
`` No , '' reply Reddy , `` but I mean to , soon . ''

In fact he have hunt and hunt for it , but have n't find a trace of it .
And all the time Sammy Jay know that Reddy do n't know where it be .
But Sammy do n't let on that he know .

`` By the way , he think you do n't know where he live now . ''
`` Huh ! ''
say Reddy Fox .
`` As if Johnny Chuck could fool me !
Well , I must be move along .
Good-by , Sammy Jay . ''
Reddy trot off towards the Green Meadows , but the minute he be out of sight of Sammy Jay , he turn towards Farmer Brown 's old orchard , just a Sammy Jay have know he would .
`` I guess Johnny Chuck will have a visitor , '' chuckle Sammy Jay , a he start to look for Jimmy Skunk .
XVII MORE MISCHIEF Mischief 's like a snowball Sent roll down a hill ; With every turn it big grows And big , big still .
Sammy Jay have start mischief by tell Reddy Fox where Johnny Chuck 's new house be .
If you have ask him , Sammy Jay would have say that he have n't tell .
All he have say be that he have happen to be up in Farmer Brown 's old orchard and so have call on Johnny Chuck in his new house .

He be n't fool for one minute , not one little minute .
He chuckle to himself a he start to look for Jimmy Skunk .
Then he change his mind .
`` I think I 'll go up to the old orchard myself ! ''
say Sammy Jay , and away he fly .
He get there first and hid in the top of a big apple-tree , where he could see all that go on .
It be n't long before he saw Reddy Fox steal out from the Green Forest and over to the old orchard .
Reddy be nervous , very nervous .
You see , it be broad daylight , and the old orchard be very near Farmer Brown 's house .
Reddy know that he ought to have wait until night , but he know that then Johnny Chuck would be fast asleep , Now , perhaps , Johnny Chuck , think that no one know where he live , would not be on watch , and he might be able to catch Johnny .
So Reddy , with one eye on Farmer Brown 's house and one eye on the watch for some sign of Johnny Chuck , stole into the old orchard .
Every few step he would stop and look and listen .
At every little noise he would start nervously .
Then Sammy Jay would chuckle under his breath .
So Reddy Fox crept and tiptoed about through the old orchard .
Every minute he grow more nervous , and every minute he grow more disappointed , for he could find no sign of Johnny Chuck 's house .
He begin to think that Sammy Jay have fool him , and the very thought make him grind his teeth .
At last he decide to give it up .
He be down in the far corner of the old orchard , close by the old stone wall now , and he get all ready to jump over the old stone wall , when he just happen to look on the other side of the big apple-tree he be under , and there be what he be look for -- Johnny Chuck 's new house !
Johnny Chuck be n't in sight , but there be the new house , and Johnny must be either inside or not far away .
Reddy grin .
It be a sly , wicked , hungry grin .
He flatten himself out in the grass behind the big apple-tree .
`` I 'll give Johnny Chuck the surprise of his life ! ''
mutter Reddy Fox under his breath .

He know that Johnny Chuck be safely inside his house , for Johnny have see Reddy when he first come into the old orchard .
And Sammy know that Johnny Chuck know that when Reddy find that new house , he would hide just a he have do .
`` Johnny Chuck wo n't come out again to-day , and there wo n't be any excitement at all , '' think Sammy Jay in disappointment , for he have hop to see a fight between Reddy Fox and Johnny Chuck .
Just then Sammy look over to Farmer Brown 's house , and there be Farmer Brown 's boy get ready to saw wood .
The imp of mischief under Sammy 's pert cap give him an idea .
He fly over to the old apple-tree , just over Reddy 's head , and begin to scream at the top of his lung .
Farmer Brown 's boy stop work and look over towards the old orchard .
`` When a jay scream like that there be usually a fox around , '' he mutter , a he unfasten Bowser the Hound .
XVIII FARMER BROWN 'S BOY MAKES A DISCOVERY Reddy Fox glare up at Sammy Jay .

he snap .

Now Sammy Jay know perfectly well that Reddy Fox have no thought of take a nap but be hide there to try to catch Johnny Chuck .
And Sammy know that Farmer Brown 's boy could hear him scream , and that he know that when Sammy scream that way it mean there be a fox about .
Sitting in the top of the apple-tree , Sammy could see Farmer Brown 's boy starting for the old orchard , with Bowser the Hound run ahead of him .
Farmer Brown 's boy have no gun , so Sammy know that no harm would come to Reddy , but that Reddy would get a dreadful scare ; and that be what Sammy want , just out of pure mischief .
So he scream louder than ever .
Reddy Fox lose his temper .
He sit up and call Sammy Jay all the bad name he could think of .
He forget where he be .
He tell Sammy Jay what he think of him and what he would do to him if ever he catch him .
Sammy Jay keep right on scream .
He make such a noise that Reddy do n't hear footstep come nearer and nearer .
Suddenly there be a great roar right behind him .
`` Bow , wow , wow !
Bow , wow , wow , wow ! ''
-- just like that .
Reddy be so frightened that he do n't even look to see where he be jump , and bump his head against the apple-tree .
Then he start for the Green Forest , with Bowser the Hound at his heel .
Sammy Jay laugh till he lose his breath and nearly tumble off his perch .
Then he fly away , still laugh .
He think it the great joke ever .
Farmer Brown 's boy have follow Bowser the Hound into the old orchard .
`` I wonder what a fox be do up here in broad daylight , '' say he , talk to himself .
`` Perhaps one of my hen have steal her nest down here , and he have find it .
I 'll have a look , anyway . ''
So he walk on down to the far corner of the old orchard , straight to the place from which he have see Reddy Fox jump .
When he get there , of course he saw Johnny Chuck 's new house right away .
`` Ho ! ''
cry Farmer Brown 's boy .
`` Brer Fox be hunt Chucks .
I 'll keep my eye on this , and if Mr. Chuck make any trouble in my garden , I 'll know where to catch him . ''
XIX JOHNNY CHUCK 'S PRIDE Ever since Farmer Brown 's boy and Reddy Fox have find his new house in the far corner of the old orchard , Johnny Chuck have be worry .
It be not that he be afraid for himself .
Oh , my , no !
Johnny Chuck felt perfectly able to take care of himself .
But there be Polly Chuck !
He be terribly afraid that something might happen to Polly Chuck .
You see she be not big and strong like him , and then Polly Chuck be apt to be careless .
So for a while Johnny Chuck worry a great deal .
But Reddy Fox do n't come again in daytime .
You see Bowser the Hound have give him such a scare that he do n't dare to .
He sometimes come at night and sniff hungrily at Johnny Chuck 's doorway , but Johnny and Polly be safe inside , and this do n't trouble them a bit .
And Farmer Brown 's boy seem to have forget all about the new house .
So after a while Johnny Chuck stop worry so much .
The fact be Johnny Chuck have something else to think about .
He have a secret .
Yes , Sir , Johnny Chuck have a secret .

You know Sammy Jay be very proud of his own handsome blue and white coat and dearly love to show it off .

`` Well , what be it , then ? ''
snap Sammy Jay .

XXII JOHNNY CHUCK IS KEPT BUSY Johnny Chuck be naturally lazy .
You see , Johnny have very simple taste and usually he be content .
He do not have to go far from his own doorstep to get all he want to eat .
He do not have to hunt for his food , a so many of the little meadow and forest people do , and so he have a great deal of time to sit on his doorstep and watch the world go by and dream pleasant daydream and grow fat .
Now people who do not have to work usually become lazy .
It be the easy habit in the world to learn and the hard to get over .
And so , because he seldom have to work , Johnny Chuck quite naturally be lazy .
But Johnny can work when there really be need of it .
No one , unless it be Digger the Badger or Miner the Mole , can dig fast than Johnny Chuck .
And when there be real need of work , Johnny work with a will .

Johnny never have forget this , and when it be really necessary that he should work , no one work hard than he do .

And now Johnny Chuck be the busy he have ever be in all his life .
If he felt lazy these beautiful spring day , he do n't have time to think about it .

XXIII THE SCHOOL IN THE OLD ORCHARD Little Foxes , little Chucks , Little Squirrels , Mice and Mink , Just like little boy and girl , Go to school to learn to think .

Of course , there never be any real danger .
Johnny be just teach them , so that when danger do come , a it surely would , sooner or later , they would know just what to do .
